connected to your WiFi network, open the app there will be two working set profiles, they work as described bellow.\r\n\r\nFront & Rear + Fast Capture : the streaming will be more stable and you can use both front and back camera but resolution is 16:10.\r\n\r\nRear + Flash + Widescreen HD: the streaming image quality and resolution will be as high as possible and will use the 16:9 aspect ratio, on devices with 512mb of ram may cause some lag.\r\n\r\nafter choosing a profile just press the white button on the center bottom of the screen, it will start the stream server, now your phone is ready to transmit its camera pictures. tap the button on the left corner at bottom of the screen to see a list of link you can use to watch the stream i recommend you use VLC, the browser links will only work with Opera and Google Chrome with these links you are able to watch the stream and take pictures from your browser and these pictues will be automatically sent to your phone camera roll.\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nTrial mode will offer you 15 connections with no time limit for test.\r\n\r\n\r\n> Take Pictures directly from your browser \r\n> Record Videos directly from your browser\r\n> Adjust Quality of image stream\r\n> Full HD for L930 and L1520, L950, L950XL\r\n> HD Stream for L920 and 1GB phones\r\n> Easily turn on/off Flash Light \r\n> Switch between rear and frontal camera\r\n> Touch to Focus \r\n\r\n# you can adapt the stream to work as a wireless webcam using some free third party software you can find more about it by going into the app's menu > help
